<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April 25, 2007,
Apple&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Apple&#148;) issued a press release regarding Apple&#146;s financial
results for its second fiscal quarter ended March 31, 2007 and a related data
sheet. A copy of Apple&#146;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1
and a copy of the related data sheet is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.2.</font></p>

in this Current Report shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section 18
of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or
incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as
amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by
specific reference in such a filing.</font></p>

<div>


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports Second Quarter
Results</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings Grow 88 Percent
Year-over-Year</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;April
25, 2007&#151;Apple&#174; today announced financial results for its fiscal 2007 second
quarter ended March 31, 2007. The Company posted revenue of $5.26 billion and
net quarterly profit of $770 million, or $.87 per diluted share. These results
compare to revenue of $4.36 billion and net quarterly profit of $410 million,
or $.47 per diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Gross margin was 35.1
percent, up from 29.8 percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales
accounted for 43 percent of the quarter&#146;s revenue.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 1,517,000
Macintosh&#174; computers and 10,549,000 iPods during the quarter, representing 36
percent growth in Macs and 24 percent growth in iPods over the year-ago
quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The Mac is clearly gaining
market share, with sales growing 36 percent&#151;more than three times the industry
growth rate,&#148; said Steve Jobs, Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;We&#146;re very excited about the
upcoming launch of iPhone in late June, and are also hard at work on some other
amazing new products in our pipeline.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are very pleased to
report the most profitable March quarter in Apple&#146;s history,&#148; said Peter
Oppenheimer, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Looking ahead to the third fiscal quarter of 2007,
we expect revenue of about $5.1&nbsp;billion and earnings per diluted share of about
$.66.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple
will provide live streaming of its Q2 2007 financial results conference call
utilizing QuickTime&#174;, Apple&#146;s standards-based technology for live and on-demand
audio and video streaming. The live webcast will begin at 2:00 p.m. PDT on
Wednesday, April 25, 2007 at www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq207/ and will
also be available for replay. The QuickTime player is available free for Macintosh
and Windows users at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\11512147729_D11851_2044606\12261-2-mm.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Apr 25 12:01 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains
forward-looking statements about the Company&#146;s estimated revenue and earnings
per share. These statements involve risks and uncertainties, and actual results
may differ. Risks and uncertainties include potential litigation and government
enforcement actions that may result from the matters investigated by the
special committee of the board of directors and the restatement of the Company&#146;s
consolidated financial statements; unfavorable results of legal proceedings;
the effect of competitive and economic factors, and the Company&#146;s reaction to
those factors, on consumer and business buying decisions with respect to the
Company&#146;s products; war, terrorism, public health issues, and other
circumstances that could disrupt supply, delivery, or demand of products;
continued competitive pressures in the marketplace;&#160; the continued availability on acceptable
terms of certain components and services essential to the Company&#146;s business
currently obtained by the Company from sole or limited sources; the ability of
the Company to make timely delivery of new programs, products and successful
technological innovations to the marketplace; the effect that product quality
problems could have on the Company&#146;s sales and operating profits; the inventory
risk associated with the Company&#146;s need to order or commit to order product
components in advance of customer orders; the effect that the Company&#146;s
dependency on manufacturing and logistics services provided by third parties
may have on the quality, quantity or cost of products manufactured or services
rendered; the Company&#146;s dependency on the performance of distributors and other
resellers of the Company&#146;s products; the Company&#146;s reliance on the availability
of third-party digital content; the potential impact of a finding that the
Company has infringed on the intellectual property rights of others; and risks
associated with the Company&#146;s retail initiative, including significant
investment cost, uncertain consumer acceptance and potential impact on existing
reseller relationships. More information on potential factors that could affect
the Company&#146;s financial results is included from time to time in the Company&#146;s
public reports filed with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for the
fiscal year ended September 30, 2006, its Form 10-Q for the quarter ended
December 30, 2006 and its Form 10-Q for the quarter ended March 31, 2007 to be
filed with the SEC. The Company assumes no obligation to update any
forward-looking statements or information, which speak as of their respective
dates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple ignited the personal
computer revolution in the 1970s with the Apple II and reinvented the personal
computer in the 1980s with the Macintosh. Today, Apple continues to
lead&nbsp;the industry in innovation with its award-winning computers, OS X
operating system and iLife and professional applications. Apple is also
spearheading the digital media revolution with its iPod portable music and
video players and iTunes online store, and will enter the mobile phone market
this year with its revolutionary iPhone.</font></p>
